‚Ä¢ Added memory-bank/Scrum/20251030-jump-into-project/76ca/20251030-2037-io-and-plan.md (+97 -0)
     1 +TL;DR
     2 +- Ship OIS MVP in 10‚Äì12 weeks: Registry/Identity-KYC, Tokenization, Custody/HSM, Settlement T+0 with 1 bank, Audit ledg
        er + Disclosure.
     3 +- Start permissioned ledger (Hyperledger Fabric/Besu) or immudb audit-core for MVP; keep path to full DLT and later DEX
        /secondary market.
     4 +- Spec-first, event-driven (Kafka), strict compliance: 259-–§–ó, KEP/–£–ö–≠–ü, AML/KYC, audit/immutability.
     5 +
     6 +Steps
     7 +1) Align scope: only primary market for MVP; secondary later (RFQ/OTC ‚Üí books).
     8 +2) C4 Context/Containers workshop (90 min) with Yury + tech lead.
     9 +3) Decide ledger: Fabric vs Besu vs immudb (audit-core), pick 1 with rollout path.
    10 +4) Define domains/events: Registry, Identity-KYC, Tokenization, Settlement, Custody, Disclosure.
    11 +5) MVP backlog + test scenarios (emission, DvP, failures, rollback).
    12 +6) Integration spike with 1 bank (payments, escrow, DvP Rails), choose HSM/MPC.
    13 +7) Build by slices: Auth/KYC ‚Üí Tokenization ‚Üí Settlement ‚Üí Audit/Reports.
    14 +8) Dry-run + UAT with synthetic data; pilot with 1 issuer.
    15 +
    16 +Why ‚Üí What ‚Üí How ‚Üí Result
    17 +- Why: Faster regulatory-grade MVP with minimal rework and BRICS-friendly stack.
    18 +- What: Permissioned OIS core with compliant issuance and atomic DvP; optional path to DEX.
    19 +- How: Spec-first (OpenAPI + event schemas), CQRS + Kafka, ledger anchoring; cloud/on-prem hardened.
    20 +- Result: Issuance live, 1 bank settlement, audit-ready logs, foundation for v1.1/v1.2.
    21 +
    22 +Architecture Snapshot (MVP)
    23 +- Gateway: OAuth2/OIDC, mTLS, WAF/anti-DDoS.
    24 +- Domains: Registry, Identity-KYC, Tokenization, Settlement-DvP, Custody/HSM, Disclosure/Reporting.
    25 +- Ledger: Fabric/Besu or immudb for audit; hash anchors; retention ‚â•7 years.
    26 +- Data: Postgres per service, S3 docs, Kafka event-log, DW for reports.
    27 +
    28 +Mermaid ‚Äî Context to Domains
    29 +```mermaid
    30 +flowchart LR
    31 +  EM[–≠–º–∏—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç] --> CAP[–ü–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞ –ö–∞–ø–∏—Ç–∞–ª ‚Äî –û–ò–° –¶–§–ê]
    32 +  INV[–ò–Ω–≤–µ—Å—Ç–æ—Ä] --> CAP
    33 +  BR[–ë—Ä–æ–∫–µ—Ä] --> CAP
    34 +  BANK[–ë–∞–Ω–∫/–ù–°–ü–ö] --> CAP

    37 +  subgraph DOM[–î–æ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å—ã]
    38 +    REGY[–†–µ–µ—Å—Ç—Ä —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤ –∏ —Ä–æ–ª–µ–π]

    57 +
    58 +Ledger Options ‚Äî Trade-offs
    59 +| Option | Pros | Cons | Fit (MVP) |
    60 +|---|---|---|---|
    61 +| Hyperledger Fabric | Mature permissioned, channels, rich ACL | Oper complexity, chaincode model | Strong if ops ready
         |
    62 +| Hyperledger Besu (permissioned) | EVM, Solidity, ecosystem tooling | Governance, privacy patterns | Good if Solidity
        talent |
    63 +| immudb (audit-core) | Simple, fast, append-only, small ops | Not smart contracts | Best for fast MVP audit |

        ater |

  3. **–†–µ–≥—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç**: –†–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç–µ –ø–æ–¥ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∞ –¶–§–ê –∏–ª–∏ —ç—Ç–æ pre-licensing research? –ï—Å—Ç—å –ª–∏ —É–∂–µ –ø–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞–Ω–∏–µ
  –ø–æ —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è–º –¶–ë –†–§ –∫ –∏–Ω—Ñ—Ä–∞—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–µ?

  –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ –≤–∞—à–∏—Ö –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç–æ–≤ –∑–∞–ø—É—â—É –≥–ª—É–±–æ–∫–æ–µ –∏—Å—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ –Ω—É–∂–Ω—ã–º –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è–º —Å —Ñ–æ–∫—É—Å–æ–º –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–µ –∫–µ–π—Å—ã 2024-2025 –∏
  —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫—É—é —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏—Ñ–∏–∫—É.
  ```


‚Ä¢ TL;DR

  - –û—Ç–≤–µ—Ç–∏–ª –Ω–∞ –≤—Å–µ 12 —É—Ç–æ—á–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–π –≤ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç–µ ‚Äú–í–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å ‚Äî –û—Ç–≤–µ—Ç‚Äù; –¥–∞–ª –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–∏–∫—É –¥–ª—è PoC –∏ —Å—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è Ledger.
  - –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –¥–ª—è –¥–∞–ª—å–Ω–µ–π—à–∏—Ö deepresearch: markdown ‚Äú–í–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å ‚Äî –û—Ç–≤–µ—Ç‚Äù + –æ–ø—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ JSON-—Å–Ω–∞–ø—à–æ—Ç –¥–ª—è –∏–º–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞.
  - –ö—É—Ä—Å: –†–§/–¶–ë, –ì–û–°–¢‚Äë—Å–æ–≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç—å ‚Äî –¥–∞; MVP –±–µ–∑ –ì–ò–°‚Äë–∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–π; PoC –¥–≤—É—Ö—Ñ–∞–∑–Ω—ã–π (Docker ‚Üí HSM/–£–ö–≠–ü).

  Steps

  1. –ó–∞—Ñ–∏–∫—Å–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—ã –Ω–∏–∂–µ –∫–∞–∫ –∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–Ω—ã–µ –¥–æ–ø—É—â–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥–ª—è PoC –∏ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã —Å—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è Ledger.
  2. –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å merged‚Äëprompts –ø–æ–¥ —ç—Ç–∏ –¥–æ–ø—É—â–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—å 2‚Äì3 —Ç–∏–∫–µ—Ç–∞ (Ledger, –£–ö–≠–ü/–ì–û–°–¢, DvP).
  3. –ü–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å PoC‚Äë–ø–ª–∞–Ω: Besu RAFT/IBFT + —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–∏ Emission/DvP/Anchoring; –º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏–∫–∏ latency/finality/ops.

  –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç

  - Markdown:
      - –í–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å ‚Äî –û—Ç–≤–µ—Ç
  - JSON (–æ–ø—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ, –¥–ª—è –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ –≤ —Ç—É–ª–∑–∏–Ω–≥):
      - { "question": "...", "answer": "...", "block": "ledger|poc|governance", "priority": 1-5 }

  –í–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å ‚Äî –û—Ç–≤–µ—Ç

  1. –ö–∞–∫–æ–π —Ç–∏–ø —é—Ä–∏—Å–¥–∏–∫—Ü–∏–∏/—Ä–µ–≥—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä–∞ –≤ —Ñ–æ–∫—É—Å–µ?
     ‚Äî –¶–ë –†–§ (259‚Äë–§–ó) –∫–∞–∫ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π —Ä–µ–≥—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä –û–ò–°/–¶–§–ê; –ø–ª—é—Å –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—É—Ä—ã –†–æ—Å—Ñ–∏–Ω–º–æ–Ω–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–Ω–≥–∞ (AML/CFT). –ú–∏–Ω—Ü–∏—Ñ—Ä—ã ‚Äî –≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—á–Ω–æ
     (–ò–¢‚Äë—Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è, –∏–º–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–æ–∑–∞–º–µ—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ).
  2. –ï—Å—Ç—å –ª–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ç –ø–æ —Å–æ–≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏ —Å –ì–û–°–¢/–§–°–ë‚Äë–∫—Ä–∏–ø—Ç–æ–≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–µ–π?
     ‚Äî –î–∞. –¢—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∞ –£–ö–≠–ü –ø–æ 63‚Äë–§–ó (–ì–û–°–¢), —Å–æ–≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç—å —Å –æ—Ç–µ—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ HSM/–°–ö–ó–ò –∏ CryptoPro/KC1/KC2 —Å—Ç–µ–∫–∞–º–∏.
  3. –ü–ª–∞–Ω–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è —Å –ì–ò–° –ì–ú–ü/–ê–° –§–¢–° –Ω–∞ MVP?
     ‚Äî –ù–µ—Ç. MVP: —ç–º–∏—Å—Å–∏—è, —É—á—ë—Ç, DvP —Å –æ–¥–Ω–∏–º –±–∞–Ω–∫–æ–º, –æ—Ç—á—ë—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å. –ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —Å –ì–ò–° ‚Äî –≤ –±—ç–∫–ª–æ–≥ (–ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –ø–µ—Ä–≤–∏—á–∫–∏).
  4. –û–±—ä—ë–º —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–π/–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π –¥–ª—è –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∏ latency?
     ‚Äî PoC —Ü–µ–ª—å: 50 tps ledger‚Äëwrite, finality 1‚Äì2 s (IBFT/RAFT), p95 end‚Äëto‚Äëend < 3‚Äì5 s; –Ω–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ API 500‚Äì800 rps. MVP —Ü–µ–ª—å:
     200 tps (–º–∞—Å—à—Ç–∞–±–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è), 10‚Äì50k –∑–∞—Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ü–∏—è 200‚Äì500 –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã—Ö.
  5. –û—Ä–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä PoC: Docker –∏–ª–∏ full‚Äëblown —Å HSM/–£–ö–≠–ü?
     ‚Äî –î–≤—É—Ö—Ñ–∞–∑–Ω–æ: Phase A ‚Äî Docker‚Äëcompose/k8s (–±–µ–∑ HSM, —ç–º—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä –ö–≠–ü). Phase B ‚Äî —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤—ã–π –£–¶ + HSM —ç–º—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä/–∞–ø–ø–ª–∏–∞–Ω—Å,
     –£–ö–≠–ü‚Äë–ø–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å–∏ –∏ TSA.
  6. –ü—Ä–∏–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ç—ã —Å—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è Ledger (—á—Ç–æ –≤–∞–∂–Ω–µ–µ)?
     ‚Äî 1) Ops‚Äë–ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–∞/—ç–∫—Å–ø–ª—É–∞—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è –∏ —É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—å, 2) Privacy‚Äë–ø–∞—Ç—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω—ã (Tessera/–∫–∞–Ω–∞–ª—ã), 3) Latency/Finality, 4) Tooling/
     —ç–∫–æ—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞.
  7. –ì–µ–æ–≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏—è PoC (–†–§/–∏–º–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–æ–∑–∞–º–µ—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ)?
     ‚Äî –î–∞, —Ü–µ–ª–µ–≤–∞—è –∏–Ω—Ñ—Ä–∞—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –≤ –†–§, —Å–∞–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–æ‚Äë–Ω–µ–π—Ç—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ OSS‚Äë–∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç—ã, —Å–æ–≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç—å —Å –æ—Ç–µ—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ HSM/–ö–°–ó–ò –∏
     RU‚Äë–æ–±–ª–∞–∫–∞–º–∏.
  8. Use‚Äëcase MVP –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–µ–Ω (Emission, DvP, Anchoring)?
     ‚Äî –î–∞: –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–µ –æ–±–ª–∏–≥–∞—Ü–∏–∏/–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∞ —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è, —ç–º–∏—Å—Å–∏—è ‚Üí —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ ‚Üí DvP T+0 ‚Üí —É—á—ë—Ç; —Ö–µ—à‚Äë–∞–Ω–∫–æ—Ä–∏–Ω–≥ –¥–ª—è –Ω–µ–∏–∑–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏.
  9. –ù—É–∂–µ–Ω –ª–∏ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–æ–ø —Å –°–ë–ü/–§–ì–ò–° –¶–§–ê –Ω–∞ MVP?
     ‚Äî –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–æ–ø —Å –°–ë–ü ‚Äî –æ–ø–æ—Å—Ä–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –±–∞–Ω–∫‚Äë–ø–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω—ë—Ä; –§–ì–ò–° –¶–§–ê ‚Äî –Ω–µ –≤ MVP, –Ω–æ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∏–º —ç–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç–æ–≤/—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏–ª–∏—â–µ —Ä–∞—Å–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–∏–π.
  10. –ö–∞–∫–æ–π –±–ª–æ–∫ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–µ–Ω –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–º –¥–ª—è MVP?
     ‚Äî –ö—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–π –ø—É—Ç—å: (1) Ledger‚Äë–≤—ã–±–æ—Ä + –∞–¥–∞–ø—Ç–µ—Ä, (2) DvP rails —Å –±–∞–Ω–∫–æ–º, (3) –£–ö–≠–ü/–ì–û–°–¢‚Äë–ø–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å–∏, (4) AML/CFT –º–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ
     –∂–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω—ã–π; –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç—ã ‚Äî –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–ª–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ.
  11. –í—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–∞–º–∫–∏ MVP?
     ‚Äî PoC 2‚Äì3 –Ω–µ–¥–µ–ª–∏; MVP 10‚Äì12 –Ω–µ–¥–µ–ª—å (–ø—Ä–∏ —Å–∫–æ—É–ø–µ ‚Äú—Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø–µ—Ä–≤–∏—á–∫–∞‚Äù); –ø–∏–ª–æ—Ç ‚Äî Q4‚Äô25/Q1‚Äô26 –≤ –∑–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –æ—Ç –±–∞–Ω–∫–∏–Ω–≥–∞/–£–ö–≠–ü
     –≤–µ–Ω–¥–æ—Ä–∞.
  12. –†–µ–≥—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç: –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä —É–∂–µ –µ—Å—Ç—å –∏–ª–∏ pre‚Äëlicensing?
     ‚Äî Pre‚Äëlicensing/–≤ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–µ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –ª–∏—Ü–µ–Ω–∑–∏–∏ –û–ò–°. –ê—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –∏ –∞—Ä—Ç–µ—Ñ–∞–∫—Ç—ã –ø–æ–¥ —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –¶–ë –†–§; —Ä–µ–≥–æ—Ç—á—ë—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å ‚Äî –±–∞–∑–æ–≤–∞—è
     –Ω–∞ MVP.

  –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ (–∫—Ä–∞—Ç–∫–∞—è –≤—ã–∂–∏–º–∫–∞)

  - –†–µ–≥—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä: –¶–ë –†–§ (259‚Äë–§–ó) + AML (–†–æ—Å—Ñ–∏–Ω–º–æ–Ω–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–Ω–≥)
  - –ì–û–°–¢/–£–ö–≠–ü: –¥–∞, –æ–±—è–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–∞ –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∞ 63‚Äë–§–ó –∏ –æ—Ç–µ—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö HSM
  - –ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ì–ò–° –Ω–∞ MVP: –Ω–µ—Ç, –≤ –±—ç–∫–ª–æ–≥
  - –ù–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ (PoC/MVP): 50/200 tps; finality 1‚Äì2 s; p95 < 3‚Äì5 s
  - PoC —Å–µ—Ç–∞–ø: Phase A Docker ‚Üí Phase B HSM/–£–ö–≠–ü
  - –ü—Ä–∏–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ç—ã —Å—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è: ops ‚Üí privacy ‚Üí latency ‚Üí tooling
  - –ì–µ–æ–≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏—è: –†–§, –∏–º–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–æ–∑–∞–º–µ—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ
  - Use‚Äëcase MVP: —ç–º–∏—Å—Å–∏—è, DvP, –∞–Ω–∫–æ—Ä–∏–Ω–≥
  - –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–æ–ø (MVP): –°–ë–ü —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –±–∞–Ω–∫; –§–ì–ò–° –¶–§–ê ‚Äî –ø–æ–∑–∂–µ
  - –ö—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–π –ø—É—Ç—å: Ledger ‚Üí DvP ‚Üí –£–ö–≠–ü ‚Üí AML
  - –°—Ä–æ–∫–∏: PoC 2‚Äì3 –Ω–µ–¥; MVP 10‚Äì12 –Ω–µ–¥
  - –ö–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç: pre‚Äëlicensing –û–ò–°

  Next actions

    (–±–∞–Ω–∫ shortlist).

‚Ä¢ Added tools/claims_indexer.py (+82 -0)
     1 +#!/usr/bin/env python3
     2 +"""
     3 +Claims Indexer
     4 +- Scans deepresearch outputs and merges any *.jsonl claims into consolidated files
     5 +- Cases supported:
     6 +  * ledger-rwa-worldwide-ru-cfa -> co-76ca/claims/ledger.claims.jsonl
     7 +  * cfa-platforms-ru-2024-2025  -> co-76ca/claims/cfa_ru.claims.jsonl
     8 +
     9 +Usage:
    10 +  python3 tools/claims_indexer.py
    11 +"""
    12 +import os, sys, json, pathlib
    13 +
    14 +ROOT = pathlib.Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]
    15 +OUT_DIR = ROOT/"memory-bank/Scrum/20251030-jump-into-project/co-76ca/claims"
    16 +
    17 +CASES = {
    18 +    'ledger': {
    19 +        'match': '00-Ledger-RWA-platforms-worldwide-and-RU-CFA-deepresearches',
    20 +        'outfile': OUT_DIR/"ledger.claims.jsonl",
    21 +    },
    22 +    'cfa_ru': {
    23 +        'match': '01-CFA-platforms-RU-2024-2025',
    24 +        'outfile': OUT_DIR/"cfa_ru.claims.jsonl",
    25 +    }
    26 +}
    27 +
    28 +SEARCH_DIRS = [
    29 +    ROOT/"memory-bank/Scrum/20251030-jump-into-project/deepresearches",
    30 +    ROOT/"memory-bank/Scrum/20251030-jump-into-project/co-76ca/deepresearch-pipelines",
    31 +]
    32 +
    33 +def iter_jsonl_files():
    34 +    for base in SEARCH_DIRS:
    35 +        if not base.exists():
    36 +            continue
    37 +        for dirpath, _, filenames in os.walk(base):
    38 +            for fn in filenames:
    39 +                if fn.endswith('.jsonl'):
    40 +                    yield pathlib.Path(dirpath)/fn
    41 +
    42 +def classify(path: pathlib.Path):
    43 +    sp = str(path)
    44 +    for key, meta in CASES.items():
    45 +        if meta['match'] in sp:
    46 +            return key
    47 +    return None
    48 +
    49 +def main():
    50 +    OUT_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    51 +    buckets = {k: [] for k in CASES}
    52 +    for p in iter_jsonl_files():
    53 +        key = classify(p)
    54 +        if key:
    55 +            buckets[key].append(p)
    56 +    for key, files in buckets.items():
    57 +        if not files:
    58 +            continue
    59 +        out = CASES[key]['outfile']
    60 +        with out.open('w', encoding='utf-8') as w:
    61 +            for f in sorted(files):
    62 +                for line in f.open('r', encoding='utf-8'):
    63 +                    line = line.strip()
    64 +                    if not line:
    65 +                        continue
    66 +                    # Minimal validation: must be JSON object
    67 +                    try:
    68 +                        obj = json.loads(line)
    69 +                    except Exception:
    70 +                        continue
    71 +                    w.write(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False)+"\n")
    72 +    # Write index file
    73 +    index = {
    74 +        'ledger': [str(p) for p in buckets['ledger']],
    75 +        'cfa_ru': [str(p) for p in buckets['cfa_ru']],
    76 +    }
    77 +    (OUT_DIR/"claims.index.json").write_text(json.dumps(index, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
    78 +    print("Indexed:", {k: len(v) for k,v in index.items()})
    79 +
    80 +if __name__ == '__main__':
    81 +    sys.exit(main())
    82 +

     15 +def parse_sources_block(lines, start_idx):
     16 +    evid = []
     17 +    i = start_idx
     18 +    while i < len(lines):
     19 +        line = lines[i].strip()
     20 +        if line.startswith('###') or line.startswith('##') or not line:
     21 +            break
     22 +        m = re.match(r"- \[(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})\] (https?://\S+)", line)
     23 +        if m:
     24 +            evid.append({"url": m.group(2), "date": m.group(1)})
     25 +        i += 1
     26 +    return evid, i
     27 +
     28 +def parse_section(lines, start_idx):
     29 +    data = {"status":"unknown","role":[],"dlt":{},"custody":{},"ukep":{},"dvp":{},
     30 +            "secondary":{},"apis":{},"hosting":{},"metrics":{},"regulatory":{},"sources":[]}
     31 +    i = start_idx
     32 +    while i < len(lines):
     33 +        line = lines[i].rstrip('\n')
     34 +        if line.startswith('## ') and i != start_idx:
     35 +            break
     36 +        # Simple field captures
     37 +        if line.startswith('**–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å:**'):
     38 +            data['status'] = line.split('**–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å:**',1)[1].strip().strip()
     39 +        if line.startswith('**–†–æ–ª–∏:**'):
     40 +            roles = line.split('**–†–æ–ª–∏:**',1)[1].strip().strip()
     41 +            data['role'] = [r.strip() for r in roles.split(',') if r.strip()]
     42 +        if line.strip() == '### DLT/Blockchain':
     43 +            # Next lines include **–¢–∏–ø:** and possibly –ò—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫–∏
     44 +            j = i+1
     45 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     46 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–¢–∏–ø:**'):
     47 +                    data.setdefault('dlt',{})['type'] = lines[j].split('**–¢–∏–ø:**',1)[1].strip().lower()
     48 +                if lines[j].strip() == '**–ò—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫–∏:**':
     49 +                    evid, j2 = parse_sources_block(lines, j+1)
     50 +                    data.setdefault('dlt',{}).setdefault('evidence',[]).extend(evid)
     51 +                    j = j2-1
     52 +                j += 1
     53 +            i = j-1
     54 +        if line.strip() == '### –£–ö–≠–ü/–ö—Ä–∏–ø—Ç–æ–≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏—è':
     55 +            j = i+1
     56 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     57 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–ì–û–°–¢:**'):
     58 +                    data.setdefault('ukep',{})['gost'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     59 +                j += 1
     60 +            i = j-1
     61 +        if line.strip() == '### DvP/–†–∞—Å—á–µ—Ç—ã':
     62 +            j = i+1
     63 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     64 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–ú–æ–¥–µ–ª—å:**'):
     65 +                    data.setdefault('dvp',{})['model'] = lines[j].split('**–ú–æ–¥–µ–ª—å:**',1)[1].strip().lower()
     66 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–ë–∞–Ω–∫–∏:**'):
     67 +                    banks = lines[j].split('**–ë–∞–Ω–∫–∏:**',1)[1].strip()
     68 +                    data.setdefault('dvp',{})['banks'] = [b.strip() for b in banks.split(',') if b.strip() and banks!=
         '-']
     69 +                if lines[j].startswith('**ISO 20022:**'):
     70 +                    data.setdefault('dvp',{})['iso20022'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     71 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–°–ë–ü:**'):
     72 +                    data.setdefault('dvp',{})['sbp'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     73 +                j += 1
     74 +            i = j-1
     75 +        if line.strip() == '### –í—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—á–Ω—ã–π —Ä—ã–Ω–æ–∫':
     76 +            j = i+1
     77 +            sec = {}
     78 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     79 +                if lines[j].startswith('**RFQ:**'):
     80 +                    sec['rfq'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     81 +                if lines[j].startswith('**Orderbook:**'):
     82 +                    sec['orderbook'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     83 +                j += 1
     84 +            data['secondary'] = sec
     85 +            i = j-1
     86 +        if line.strip() == '### API/–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è':
     87 +            j = i+1
     88 +            apis = {}
     89 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     90 +                if lines[j].startswith('**OpenAPI:**'):
     91 +                    apis['openapi'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     92 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è:**'):
     93 +                    doc_url = lines[j].split('**–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è:**',1)[1].strip()
     94 +                    apis['docs'] = [doc_url] if doc_url and doc_url!='-' else []
     95 +                j += 1
     96 +            data['apis'] = apis
     97 +            i = j-1
     98 +        if line.strip() == '### –†–µ–≥—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω—ã–π —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å':
     99 +            j = i+1
    100 +            reg = {}
    101 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
    102 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–õ–∏—Ü–µ–Ω–∑–∏–∏:**'):
    103 +                    val = lines[j].split('**–õ–∏—Ü–µ–Ω–∑–∏–∏:**',1)[1].strip()
    104 +                    reg['licenses'] = [s.strip() for s in val.split(',') if s.strip()]
    105 +                j += 1
    106 +            data['regulatory'] = reg
    107 +            i = j-1
    108 +        i += 1
    109 +    return data, i
    110 +
    111 +def main():
    112 +    text = SRC.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    113 +    lines = text.splitlines()
    114 +    # Build index of sections
    115 +    sections = {}
    116 +    for idx,line in enumerate(lines):
    117 +        if line.startswith('## '):
    118 +            title = line[3:].strip()
    119 +            sections[title] = idx
    120 +    out_cards = []
    121 +    for target in TARGETS:
    122 +        # find matching section (exact or startswith)
    123 +        key = None
    124 +        for t in sections:
    125 +            if t == target or t.startswith(target):
    126 +                key = t
    127 +                break
    128 +        if not key:
    129 +            continue
    130 +        data, _ = parse_section(lines, sections[key])
    131 +        card = {
    132 +            'name': key,
    133 +            **{k:v for k,v in data.items() if v}
    134 +        }
    135 +        out_cards.append(card)
    136 +    # write JSONL
    137 +    OUT_JSONL.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    138 +    with OUT_JSONL.open('w', encoding='utf-8') as w:
    139 +        for c in out_cards:
    140 +            w.write(json.dumps(c, ensure_ascii=False)+"\n")
    141 +    # write MD summary
    142 +    with OUT_MD.open('w', encoding='utf-8') as w:
    143 +        w.write('---\ncreated: 2025-10-31 10:56\nupdated: 2025-10-31 10:56\n')
    144 +        w.write('type: research-summary\nsphere: [market, cfa]\n')
    145 +        w.write('topic: [competitors]\nauthor: codex\n')
    146 +        w.write('agentID: 019a362f-76ca-7272-909e-362716cf233d\npartAgentID: [co-76ca]\nversion: 1.0.0\ntags: [summary
         , competitors]\n---\n\n')
    147 +        w.write('TL;DR\n- –°–æ–±—Ä–∞–Ω–æ {} –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–µ–∫ (Batch‚Äë1).\n\n'.format(len(out_cards)))
    148 +        w.write('| –ü–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞ | DLT | DvP | RFQ | Orderbook | OpenAPI | Licenses |\n')
    149 +        w.write('|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|\n')
    150 +        for c in out_cards:
    151 +            dlt = c.get('dlt',{}).get('type','unknown')
    152 +            dvp = c.get('dvp',{}).get('model','unknown')
    153 +            rfq = str(c.get('secondary',{}).get('rfq')) if 'secondary' in c else 'unknown'
    154 +            ob = str(c.get('secondary',{}).get('orderbook')) if 'secondary' in c else 'unknown'
    155 +            openapi = str(c.get('apis',{}).get('openapi')) if 'apis' in c else 'unknown'
    156 +            lic = ','.join(c.get('regulatory',{}).get('licenses',[]))
    157 +            w.write(f"| {c['name']} | {dlt} | {dvp} | {rfq} | {ob} | {openapi} | {lic} |\n")
    158 +    print(f"Wrote {len(out_cards)} cards to {OUT_JSONL} and summary to {OUT_MD}")

    161 +    sys.exit(main())

  - Perplexity ‚Äî JSONL + –ø–æ–¥—Ä–æ–±–Ω—ã–µ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫–∏; Coverage: –≤—ã—Å–æ–∫–∏–π, Novelty: –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–π, Actionability: —Å—Ä–µ–¥–Ω–∏–π. Verdict: –æ–±—è–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–Ω
    –∫–∞–∫ source‚Äëheavy.

    ‚Äî –∏–∑–±—ã—Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ.

‚Ä¢ Added tools/make_competitors_from_sources_all.py (+142 -0)
      1 +#!/usr/bin/env python3
      2 +import re, json, pathlib, sys
      3 +
      4 +SRC = pathlib.Path('memory-bank/Scrum/20251030-jump-into-project/deepresearches/01-CFA-platforms-RU-2024-2025/20251008
         30-perplexity.deepresearch/competitors-sources.md')
      5 +OUT_JSONL = pathlib.Path('memory-bank/Scrum/20251030-jump-into-project/co-76ca/competitors_all.jsonl')
      6 +OUT_MD = pathlib.Path('memory-bank/Scrum/20251030-jump-into-project/co-76ca/competitors_all.md')
      7 +
      8 +def parse_sources_block(lines, start_idx):
      9 +    evid = []
     10 +    i = start_idx
     11 +    while i < len(lines):
     12 +        line = lines[i].strip()
     13 +        if line.startswith('###') or line.startswith('##') or not line:
     14 +            break
     15 +        m = re.match(r"- \[(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})\] (https?://\S+)", line)
     16 +        if m:
     17 +            evid.append({"url": m.group(2), "date": m.group(1)})
     18 +        i += 1
     19 +    return evid, i
     20 +
     21 +def parse_section(lines, start_idx):
     22 +    data = {"status":"unknown","role":[],"dlt":{},"custody":{},"ukep":{},"dvp":{},
     23 +            "secondary":{},"apis":{},"hosting":{},"metrics":{},"regulatory":{},"sources":[]}
     24 +    i = start_idx
     25 +    while i < len(lines):
     26 +        line = lines[i].rstrip('\n')
     27 +        if line.startswith('## ') and i != start_idx:
     28 +            break
     29 +        if line.startswith('**–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å:**'):
     30 +            data['status'] = line.split('**–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å:**',1)[1].strip()
     31 +        if line.startswith('**–†–æ–ª–∏:**'):
     32 +            roles = line.split('**–†–æ–ª–∏:**',1)[1].strip()
     33 +            data['role'] = [r.strip() for r in roles.split(',') if r.strip()]
     34 +        if line.strip() == '### DLT/Blockchain':
     35 +            j = i+1
     36 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     37 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–¢–∏–ø:**'):
     38 +                    data.setdefault('dlt',{})['type'] = lines[j].split('**–¢–∏–ø:**',1)[1].strip().lower()
     39 +                if lines[j].strip() == '**–ò—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫–∏:**':
     40 +                    evid, j2 = parse_sources_block(lines, j+1)
     41 +                    data.setdefault('dlt',{}).setdefault('evidence',[]).extend(evid)
     42 +                    j = j2-1
     43 +                j += 1
     44 +            i = j-1
     45 +        if line.strip() == '### –£–ö–≠–ü/–ö—Ä–∏–ø—Ç–æ–≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏—è':
     46 +            j = i+1
     47 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     48 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–ì–û–°–¢:**'):
     49 +                    data.setdefault('ukep',{})['gost'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     50 +                j += 1
     51 +            i = j-1
     52 +        if line.strip() == '### DvP/–†–∞—Å—á–µ—Ç—ã':
     53 +            j = i+1
     54 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     55 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–ú–æ–¥–µ–ª—å:**'):
     56 +                    data.setdefault('dvp',{})['model'] = lines[j].split('**–ú–æ–¥–µ–ª—å:**',1)[1].strip().lower()
     57 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–ë–∞–Ω–∫–∏:**'):
     58 +                    banks = lines[j].split('**–ë–∞–Ω–∫–∏:**',1)[1].strip()
     59 +                    data.setdefault('dvp',{})['banks'] = [b.strip() for b in banks.split(',') if b.strip() and banks!=
         '-']
     60 +                if lines[j].startswith('**ISO 20022:**'):
     61 +                    data.setdefault('dvp',{})['iso20022'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     62 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–°–ë–ü:**'):
     63 +                    data.setdefault('dvp',{})['sbp'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     64 +                j += 1
     65 +            i = j-1
     66 +        if line.strip() == '### –í—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—á–Ω—ã–π —Ä—ã–Ω–æ–∫':
     67 +            j = i+1
     68 +            sec = {}
     69 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     70 +                if lines[j].startswith('**RFQ:**'):
     71 +                    sec['rfq'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     72 +                if lines[j].startswith('**Orderbook:**'):
     73 +                    sec['orderbook'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     74 +                j += 1
     75 +            data['secondary'] = sec
     76 +            i = j-1
     77 +        if line.strip() == '### API/–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è':
     78 +            j = i+1
     79 +            apis = {}
     80 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     81 +                if lines[j].startswith('**OpenAPI:**'):
     82 +                    apis['openapi'] = '–î–∞' in lines[j]
     83 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è:**'):
     84 +                    doc_url = lines[j].split('**–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è:**',1)[1].strip()
     85 +                    apis['docs'] = [doc_url] if doc_url and doc_url!='-' else []
     86 +                j += 1
     87 +            data['apis'] = apis
     88 +            i = j-1
     89 +        if line.strip() == '### –†–µ–≥—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω—ã–π —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å':
     90 +            j = i+1
     91 +            reg = {}
     92 +            while j < len(lines) and not lines[j].startswith('###') and not lines[j].startswith('##'):
     93 +                if lines[j].startswith('**–õ–∏—Ü–µ–Ω–∑–∏–∏:**'):
     94 +                    val = lines[j].split('**–õ–∏—Ü–µ–Ω–∑–∏–∏:**',1)[1].strip()
     95 +                    reg['licenses'] = [s.strip() for s in val.split(',') if s.strip()]
     96 +                j += 1
     97 +            data['regulatory'] = reg
     98 +            i = j-1
     99 +        i += 1
    100 +    return data, i
    101 +
    102 +def main():
    103 +    text = SRC.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    104 +    lines = text.splitlines()
    105 +    sections = {}
    106 +    for idx,line in enumerate(lines):
    107 +        if line.startswith('## '):
    108 +            title = line[3:].strip()
    109 +            if title and not title.lower().startswith('–≤—Å–µ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫–∏'):
    110 +                sections[title] = idx
    111 +    out_cards = []
    112 +    for title, idx in sections.items():
    113 +        data, _ = parse_section(lines, idx)
    114 +        card = {'name': title}
    115 +        for k,v in data.items():
    116 +            if v not in (None, {}, [], ''):
    117 +                card[k]=v
    118 +        out_cards.append(card)
    119 +    OUT_JSONL.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    120 +    with OUT_JSONL.open('w', encoding='utf-8') as w:
    121 +        for c in out_cards:
    122 +            w.write(json.dumps(c, ensure_ascii=False)+"\n")
    123 +    with OUT_MD.open('w', encoding='utf-8') as w:
    124 +        w.write('---\ncreated: 2025-10-31 11:18\nupdated: 2025-10-31 11:18\n')
    125 +        w.write('type: research-summary\nsphere: [market, cfa]\n')
    126 +        w.write('topic: [competitors]\nauthor: codex\n')
    127 +        w.write('agentID: 019a362f-76ca-7272-909e-362716cf233d\npartAgentID: [co-76ca]\nversion: 1.0.0\ntags: [summary
         , competitors]\n---\n\n')
    128 +        w.write(f'TL;DR\n- –°–æ–±—Ä–∞–Ω–æ {len(out_cards)} –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–µ–∫ –∏–∑ structured sources.\n\n')
    129 +        w.write('| –ü–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞ | DLT | DvP | RFQ | Orderbook | OpenAPI | Licenses |\n|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|\n')
    130 +        for c in out_cards:
    131 +            dlt = c.get('dlt',{}).get('type','unknown')
    132 +            dvp = c.get('dvp',{}).get('model','unknown')
    133 +            rfq = str(c.get('secondary',{}).get('rfq')) if 'secondary' in c else 'unknown'
    134 +            ob = str(c.get('secondary',{}).get('orderbook')) if 'secondary' in c else 'unknown'
    135 +            openapi = str(c.get('apis',{}).get('openapi')) if 'apis' in c else 'unknown'
    136 +            lic = ','.join(c.get('regulatory',{}).get('licenses',[]))
    137 +            w.write(f"| {c['name']} | {dlt} | {dvp} | {rfq} | {ob} | {openapi} | {lic} |\n")
    138 +    print(f"Wrote {len(out_cards)} cards to {OUT_JSONL} and summary to {OUT_MD}")
    139 +
    140 +if __name__ == '__main__':
    141 +    sys.exit(main())
    142 +

  –°–≤–æ–¥–∫–∞ –ø–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞–º –∏ —Ü–µ–ª–µ—Å–æ–æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ (–Ω–∞ –±—É–¥—É—â–µ–µ)

  # Part 2
  –Ø –∏–º–µ—é –≤ –≤–∏–¥—É, —á—Ç–æ —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–æ, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –≤—ã –æ—Ä–∫–µ—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç–µ –ò–ò-–∞–≥–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –∫–∞–∫ –±–æ–≥, –∫–∞–∫ —è, —ç—Ç–æ —á–µ–ª–æ–≤–µ–∫ –∫–∞–∫ —è. –ù–æ —è –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω –±—ã—Ç—å

  –° –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã, —ç—Ç–æ –¥–µ–Ω—å–≥–∏ –æ—Ç–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å. –ú–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –µ–º—É, –Ω—É, —Ç–∏–ø–∞, –Ω–∞–∫–∏–¥—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫ –≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç–æ—Ç –Ω–∞–∑–≤–∞–ª,

  —Ç–∞–º, –∏ –≤ 3 —Ä–∞–∑–∞ –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–µ–µ. –ü–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ, –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç–µ, —è –∑–Ω–∞—é, —è –∏ –∫–æ–¥–∏–Ω–≥. –≠—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫–∏–µ, –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã, —Å–∫–∞–∑–∫–∏-–ø—Ä–∏—Å–∫–∞–∑–∫–∏. –Ø –º–æ–≥—É, –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã,

  –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å, –Ω—É, —Ç–∏–ø–∞, –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –Ω–∞ –Ω—ë–º". –¢–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å, –æ–Ω —Ö–æ—Ç–µ–ª —É–∑–Ω–∞—Ç—å –ø–æ –ø–æ–≤–æ–¥—É –º–æ–µ–π —Ä–æ–ª–∏ –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ.

  –ù–∞–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–æ–µ, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª–æ–º–Ω—ã–π –ø–µ—Ä–∏–æ–¥ –∏ –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç—å: "–°–ª—É—à–∞–π, —É –º–µ–Ω—è —Ä–æ–ª—å –∏—Å—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å, –∞—É–¥–∏—Ç–æ—Ä, –∞—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä, —Ç–≤–æ—ë
  –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –ª–∏—Ü–æ, –Ω—É, —Ç–∏–ø–∞, –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–æ–ª–∏—Ä—É—é—â–∏–π —ç—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–æ. –ù–æ —è –º–æ–≥—É –ø–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç—å—Å—è, –∏–Ω–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ø–æ–º–æ—á—å —Ä—É–∫–∞–º–∏. –ù–æ, –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, —É –º–µ–Ω—è –µ—Å—Ç—å
  –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞. –Ø –Ω–µ —Ö–æ—á—É –±—Ä–∞—Ç—å —Å–ª–∏—à–∫–æ–º –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Ä–æ–ª–µ–π. –ù–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, —É —Ç–µ–±—è –≤—Å—ë —Ä–∞–≤–Ω–æ —è –±—É–¥—É –±—Ä–∞—Ç—å 2-3 —Ä–æ–ª–∏".

  –ò—Ç–∞–∫, –∞ –µ—â—ë –∏ –¥—É—ç—Ä, —ç—Ç–æ –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã... –í–æ—Ç, —è –±—É–¥—É –¥—É—ç—Ä –≤ —Ä–æ–ª–∏ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞, –∏—Å—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è, –∞—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∞. –ò –º–æ–≥—É –≤–∑—è—Ç—å —Ä–æ–ª—å –Ω–µ –¥–µ–π–ª–∏-
  –º–µ–Ω–µ–¥–∂–µ—Ä–∞, –∞ –≤–æ—Ç —Ç–∞–∫–æ–≥–æ –ø–µ—Ä–∏–æ–¥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ. –Ø –±—ã –Ω–µ —Ö–æ—Ç–µ–ª —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π, —Ç–∏–ø–∞, –¥–µ–π–ª–∏. –ù—É, —ç—Ç–æ –≤–æ—Ç –∫–∞–∫-—Ç–æ –µ–º—É —Ç–∞–∫ –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è.

  –ò –º–Ω–µ –≤–æ—Ç —Ç–∞–∫ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å–Ω–æ. –¢–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å, —à–∞–Ω—Å—ã, –≤–æ—Ç, —á—Ç–æ —Ç–µ–±—è —Ü–µ–Ω–∏–ª–∏ 6 —Ç—ã—Å—è—á —á–∞—Å–æ–≤, –Ω–∞ —Å–∞–º–æ–º –¥–µ–ª–µ, –µ—Å—Ç–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ, —Ç—ã –º–æ–∂–µ—à—å —Ç—É—Ç,
  –∫–æ–Ω–µ—á–Ω–æ, —è —Ç–µ–±–µ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥—É... –Ø –≤–æ—Ç —Å–∫–∞–∂—É —á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ, –º—ã —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ–º –Ω–µ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –≥–æ–¥, –º—ã —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–ª–∏ 2 –≥–æ–¥–∞ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–µ. –ú—ã –∑–Ω–∞–µ–º
  –¥—Ä—É–≥ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∞ 6 –ª–µ—Ç. –ò –≤ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–∏—Ö –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞—Ö, –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç–∞—Ö –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–ª–∏. –¢—ã –∑–Ω–∞–µ—à—å, –∫–∞–∫ —è —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é, —Ç—ã –ø–æ–º–Ω–∏—à—å, –∫–∞–∫ —è –±—ã–ª –≤
  –æ—Ñ–∏—Å–µ –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ.

  –ß–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ, –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å, –Ω–∞–º –ø–æ–≤–µ–∑—ë—Ç. –ï—Å—Ç–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ, –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–π —à–∞–≥ –±—É–¥–µ–º –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –Ω–∞–∏–ª—É—á—à–∏–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–º. –ú–æ–∂–µ–º –µ—â—ë –≥–¥–µ-—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –∫–∞–∫–æ–π-—Ç–æ
  –∫–æ–Ω—Å–µ–Ω—Å—É—Å, –æ–±—Å—É–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ. –ï—Å–ª–∏ —á–µ–ª–æ–≤–µ–∫ —Ç–∞–º –∑–Ω–∞–µ—Ç –ª—É—á—à–µ, –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å, –Ω–µ –º–æ—ë —Ç–∞–º –∏–¥–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ. –ù–æ —è –≤—Å–µ–≥–¥–∞ —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–∞—é—Å—å, –¥–∞ –∏
  –±–µ—Å—Ç.

  –ù–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, –≤–æ—Ç –º—ã —Ö–æ—Ç–∏–º –∫–∞–∫—É—é-—Ç–æ –±–∏—Ä–∂—É –∏–ª–∏ –∫–∞–∫ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –ø–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É –∏–ª–∏ –∫–∞–±–∏–Ω–µ—Ç. –ù—É, –≤–æ—Ç –ª—É—á—à–∏–π —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π —è –≤–∏–∂—É, —ç—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–º
  –Ω–∞—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –æ–≥—Ä–æ–º–Ω–æ–µ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–π, —Å–æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç—å –¥–∏–∑–∞–π–Ω–æ–≤, –Ω–∞–∏—Å—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤, –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ, –∏ —Ç–∞–∫
  –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ. –ò —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–æ—Ç–∏–ø —Ñ—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω–¥–∞ –≤ Loveable –∏–ª–∏ —Ç–∞–º, –Ω—É, Word, –Ω—É, –∏–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–æ—á–∏–µ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–µ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å—ã. –í—Å—ë, —É –Ω–∞—Å –µ—Å—Ç—å –∫
  —á–µ–º—É –ø—Ä–∏–≤—è–∑—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è. –î–∞–ª—å—à–µ —Ä—É—á–∫–∏. –ú—ã –∏–¥—ë–º –∫–∞–∫ –±—É–¥—Ç–æ –æ—Ç UX.

  –ù–µ –∑–Ω–∞–µ—à—å, –∫–∞–∫ —Å—É–ø–µ—Ä —Ç–∞–º —Å—Ö–µ–º—ã –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª–∏, –∞ —á—Ç–æ –µ—â—ë —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ —Ç–∏–ø–∞ –∫—Ä—É—Ç–æ –ø–æ—â—É–ø–∞—Ç—å –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ. –ù–æ —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –æ–∑–Ω–∞—á–∞–µ—Ç, —á—Ç–æ
  —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–Ω–æ 90% —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ –≤–∏–∑—É–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞—è —á–∞—Å—Ç—å –∫–∞–∂–µ—Ç—Å—è, –∞, –≤—Å—ë —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–Ω–æ. –ù—É, –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã, –Ω–∏—Ö—É—è –Ω–∞ —Å–∞–º–æ–º –¥–µ–ª–µ, –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å, —ç—Ç–æ
  —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≤–µ—Ä—à–∏–Ω–∞ –∞–π—Å–±–µ—Ä–≥–∞. –¢—ã –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω —ç—Ç–æ –æ—Å–æ–∑–Ω–∞–≤–∞—Ç—å.

  –°–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–µ–µ –ø–æ –ø–æ–≤–æ–¥—É, —Ç–∞–º, –±–ª–æ–∫—á–µ–π–Ω–∞. –ú–æ–∂–µ—Ç, –º—ã –∞-–ª—è Docker Compose Up –∏ –¥–æ–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏–ª–∏, –∏ –æ–Ω–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç. –ê –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º, —Ç–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å, —Å–≤–µ—Ä—Ö
  –ø—Ä–æ–¥–≤–∏–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ. –ê –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç—É —à—Ç—É–∫—É —Å–≤—è–∑–∞—Ç—å, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç, –Ω—É, –ø—Ä—è–º –ø–æ—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–∏—Ç—å 30% —É—Å–∏–ª–∏–π, 40%. –•–æ—Ç—è, –∫–∞–∂–µ—Ç—Å—è, —á—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–º
  —Å–≤—è–∑–∞—Ç—å –¥–≤–µ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã.

  –í–æ–æ–±—â–µ, –≤–æ –º–Ω–æ–≥–∏—Ö –≤–µ—â–∞—Ö –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –∫–∞–∫ —Ä–∞–∑-—Ç–∞–∫–∏, –∫–∞–∫ –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–º–∞—Ç—å, —Ç–∞–º, –ª–æ–≥–∏–∫—É, –∫–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∏–∑—É—á–∏—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–∞–º —Å—Ç–æ–∏—Ç –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å,
  –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ —É –Ω–∞—Å –Ω—é–∞–Ω—Å—ã, –∏ —Ç–∏–ø–∞ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å. –û—á–µ–Ω—å –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≤—Å–µ–≥–¥–∞ –≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç–∏—Ö –∏—Å—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–π, —Ç–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å, –∏ —É –º–µ–Ω—è –±—É–¥–µ—Ç —Ç–∞–∫ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å —Å
  –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–æ–π.

  –°–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —á–µ–ª–æ–≤–µ–∫ –≤ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–µ, —Ç—ã, –Ω–∞–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–æ–µ, —Ö–æ—á–µ—à—å —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç—å?
  –°–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–µ–Ω–µ–≥ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ?
  –°–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ?

  –Ø —Ç–µ–±–µ –∏–¥–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ—Ç –≤–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å –Ω–µ –æ—Ç–≤–µ—á—É. –ù–æ –º—ã –º–æ–∂–µ–º –∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è–º–∏ –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏ –ø—Ä–∏–∫–∏–¥—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å.

  –ù–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, —á—Ç–æ —É —Ç–µ–±—è –≤–æ–æ–±—â–µ –≥–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –≤ —ç—Ç–æ–π —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–µ —É —Ç–µ–±—è —Å—É–ø–µ—Ä-–ø—É–ø–µ—Ä –ø–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞, —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –≤–æ—Ç —Ñ—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω–¥, –≥–¥–µ –≤—Å–µ –ª—é–¥–∏
  –∑–∞—Ö–æ–¥—è—Ç –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ. –ü–æ–¥ –∫–∞–ø–æ—Ç–æ–º —Ç–∞–º –æ–≥—Ä–æ–º–Ω—ã–µ –º–æ–¥—É–ª–∏. –≠—Ç–æ –º—ã –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏–ª–∏ –Ω–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–≤–æ–º –∑–≤–æ–Ω–∫–µ. –ò –≤ —Ü–µ–ª–æ–º, –∏ —Ç–∞–∫, –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –≤–æ—Ç, –∏ –≤
  —ç—Ç–æ–π –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–µ —è—Å–Ω–æ –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ. –ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –¥–∞, —Ç–∞–º, —Å –±–∞–Ω–∫–∏. –ù—É, –º–∏–∫—Ä–æ—Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è.

  –ò —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç —Å –±–∞–Ω–∫–æ–º —Å–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–æ. –ò –ø–ª—é—Å –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è. –¢–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫–æ–π-—Ç–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç —Å –±–∞–Ω–∫–æ–º, –¥–∞, –∏ –µ–≥–æ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è
  –Ω–µ–ø–æ—Å—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Å –±–∞–Ω–∫–æ–º, –¥–∞, —Ç–∞–º, –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ. –ü–æ–ø—Ä–∞–≤—å –º–µ–Ω—è, –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å, –≥–¥–µ-—Ç–æ.

  –ë–ª–æ–∫—á–µ–π–Ω —Ç–æ –∂–µ —Å–∞–º–æ–µ, —Ç–∞–º, –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —ç–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç–∏ –ø–æ –ø–æ–≤–æ–¥—É –±–∏—Ä–∂–∏ –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ, –ø–æ –ø–æ–≤–æ–¥—É —Ç–∞–º, KYC –∏ –ø—Ä–æ—á–µ–µ. –ö–∞–∫–∏–µ-—Ç–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å—ã,
  –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –≤—Å—ë —ç—Ç–æ –≤–∞–ª–∏–¥–∏—Ä—É—é—Ç, –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å, –¥–æ–¥–µ–ª—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø–æ —à–∞–≥—É - –¥–æ—Ä–æ–≥—É –æ—Å–∏–ª–∏—Ç –∏–¥—É—â–∏–π.

  –°–∫–æ—Ä–µ–µ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ, —Ç–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å, –≤–æ—Ç –º—ã —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª–∏–ª–∏ –ø–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞, –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª–∏–ª–∏ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–π value, –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã, –¥–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç—ã, –¥–µ–Ω—å–≥–∏, –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è
  —Å –±–∞–Ω–∫–æ–º. –í—ã–¥–µ–ª–∏–ª–∏ –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–π value –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç–∏—Ö –≤—Å–µ—Ö —Å—É—â–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–µ–π. –ò –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –µ—â—ë KYC —ç—Ç–∏—Ö —Å—É—â–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–µ–π, –¥–∞, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º —Å–∞–º–∏
  –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤—ã, –∫–∞–∫ —Ç–∞–º –∫–∞–∫–∞—è-—Ç–æ –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å-–ª–æ–≥–∏–∫–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç, —Å–∞–º –±–ª–æ–∫—á–µ–π–Ω –∫–∞–∫-—Ç–æ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è, –¥–∞, —Ç–∞–º.

  –ö—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏, –¥–∞, —á—Ç–æ —è –µ—â—ë –º–æ–≥—É –Ω–∞ —Å–µ–±—è —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ –≤–∑—è—Ç—å, –Ω–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã—Ö —ç—Ç–∞–ø–∞—Ö, –Ω–æ, –Ω–æ —á—Ç–æ, –∞ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –∏ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã—Ö. –ò —ç—Ç–æ —É–∂–µ
  –∏–Ω—Ñ—Ä–∞—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–Ω–∞—è —á–∞—Å—Ç—å –≤—ã—à–µ –∫—Ä—ã—à–∏ –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–æ–π, —Ç–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å, –Ω–∞ –º–Ω–µ. –î–∞, DevOps, Ops –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è. –¢–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≤–æ—Ç security –∏ –±–µ–∑–æ–ø–∞—Å–Ω–∏–∫ –Ω–∞–º
  –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω –∫–∞–∫–æ–π-—Ç–æ –µ—â—ë –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º.

  –ü–æ—á–µ–º—É –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º? –ü–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ —è –Ω–µ —Ö–æ—á—É –ø–æ –≤—Å–µ–º —Ñ—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–º –Ω–µ –≤–∑–æ—Ä–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è, –Ω–µ –ª–æ–ø–Ω—É—Ç—å –æ—Ç –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ —Ä–∞–∑, –ø–æ–¥—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ö–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ—é –∂–æ–ø—É
  –∏ —Ä–∏—Å–∫–∏. –ò –≤ —Ü–µ–ª–æ–º, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ —É —Ç–µ–±—è —Å–ª–∏—à–∫–æ–º –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≤–µ—â–µ–π –≤ –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–µ, —Ç—ã –º–æ–∂–µ—à—å –∫–∞–∫–∏—Ö-—Ç–æ –∑–∞–±—ã—Ç—å. –≠—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ, –∫–æ—Ä–æ—á–µ, —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª—è—Ç—å
  —Ä–æ–ª–∏.

  –ö–æ–≥–¥–∞ —Ç–∞–º –ø–æ—è–≤—è—Ç—Å—è –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ-—Ç–æ –¥–µ–Ω—å–≥–∏ –∏ –ø—Ä–æ—á–µ–µ. –í–µ–∑–¥–µ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –±—Ä–∞—Ç—å, –∫–æ–Ω—Å—É–ª—å—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –ª—é–¥–µ–π —Å –æ–ø—ã—Ç–æ–º, –∫—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–º —É–∂–µ –¥–µ–ª–∞–ª,
  –≤—ã–¥–≤–∏–≥–∞–ª.

  –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞-—Ç–æ –≤ 2020 –≥–æ–¥—É, –∞ –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ —è –Ω–∞ –ø–æ—á–∞—Å–æ–≤–∫–µ, –æ–Ω –±–æ–ª–µ–µ –æ—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–∂–µ–Ω –∫ —Ä–∞—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∞–º.


  –ú–æ–≥—É –∑–∞–ø—É—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—å —Ç–æ—á–µ—á–Ω—ã–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç—ã –ø–æ MECE-—à–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω–∞–º –∏ —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É —Å–æ–æ–±—â–∏—Ç—å, –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–∏—Ç—å weekly report, –¥–∞, –≤—Å–µ —ç—Ç–æ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –∏
  –æ–±—è–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –∫–æ–º–º–∏—Ç–∏—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ–π –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–π —à–∞–≥.


  –Ø —Ç—É—Ç —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –µ—â–µ —á–∏—Ç–∞—é –∏ –ø–æ–Ω—è–ª, —á—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –±—ã–ª–æ –∞–∫—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –Ω–∞—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–æ –ø–æ —Å—É—Ç–∏ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–Ω–∞ –≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç–∞ –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∞ —É –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
  –¥–æ –∞—É—Ç—Å–æ—Ä—Å-–∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏–∏. –Ø –∂–µ —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª, —á—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–º –≤ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø–µ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ –≥—Ä–∞–º–æ—Ç–Ω–æ, –∏ –Ω–∞—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –º—ã –ª—É—á—à–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–ª–∏. –ê —Ç–æ –≤–æ—Ç
  –∫–∞–∫-—Ç–æ –º—ã —Ç—É—Ç –Ω–∞ —Ñ–æ—Ä—à–º–∞—Ç–µ –∏–ª–∏ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ –≤–æ—Ç.

  –ù—É –∏ —á–∞—Å—Ç—å 2, –ª–∏–≤–µ—Ä –±–æ—Å—Å, –¥–∞ —Ç–∞–º –æ—Ç—Ç—É–¥–∞ —Ç–∏–ø–∞ —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–µ —à–∞–≥–∏, –±–æ–ª–µ–µ –¥–µ—Ç–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –¥–æ–∫–æ–≤. –í–æ–æ–±—â–µ –µ–º—É —Ö–æ—á—É —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ —Å–ª—É—à–∞–π,
  –Ω—É –≤–æ—Ç –∑–∞ —ç—Ç–∏ —á–∞—Å—ã, —á—Ç–æ –¥–∞–ª—å—à–µ –ø–æ–≥—Ä—É–∑–∏–ª–∏—Å—å, —ç—Ç–æ –∫–∞–∫ –ª—É–∫–æ–≤–∏—Ü–∞ –∏–ª–∏ –∫–∞–ø—É—Å—Ç–∞ ‚Äî –ø–æ—Å—Ç–µ–ø–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Ä–∞—Å–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—à—å, —Ä–∞—Å–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—à—å –≤—Å–µ, –Ω—É —Ç–∏–ø–∞
  –≥–ª—É–±–∂–µ, –≥–ª—É–±–∂–µ –∏–¥–µ—à—å. –ò –Ω—É —Ñ—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç –≤–æ—Ç —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π-—Ç–æ.

  –î–∞–∂–µ –Ω–µ –±—É–¥—É –µ–º—É –∞–∫—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤–Ω–∏–º–∞–Ω–∏–µ, —á—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫–∞—è –∂–µ –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∞, –∫–∞–∫ —É —Ç–µ—Ö —Ä–µ–±—è—Ç, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ –ø–æ —Ñ–∞–∫—Ç—É –∏–∑ —Ç–æ–≥–æ, —á—Ç–æ —è –≤–∏–∂—É
  —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –≤ —Ç–æ–π –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–µ —É –∞—É—Ç—Å–æ—Ä—Å-–∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏–∏ (estimation), —Ç–∞–º –≤—Å–µ —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–Ω–æ, –ø—Ä—è–º –≤–æ—Ç. –ù—É —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ –º—ã —Å–µ—Ä—á–∏–ª–∏, –¥–µ–ª–∞–ª–∏, –∏–ª–∏ —ç—Ç–æ
  –º—ã –Ω–∞ –Ω–∏—Ö –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤—ã–≤–∞–ª–∏—Å—å ‚Äî —è –Ω–µ –ø–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞—é. –í–æ—Ç —ç—Ç–æ, –∫—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏, –∑–∞–∫–æ–≤—ã—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—ã–π –≤–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å: –Ω–µ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤—ã–≤–∞–ª—Å—è –ª–∏ —Ç—ã –Ω–∞ –Ω–∏—Ö, –∞ –¥—É–º–∞–ª –ª–∏ —Ç—ã
  —Å–≤–æ–µ–π –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–æ–π –Ω–∞–∏–ª—É—á—à–∏–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–º, –Ω–µ –±—ã–ª –ª–∏ —Ç—ã –±–∞–π–∞—Å–µ–¥? –ü–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ –Ω—É –≤—Å–µ –≥—Ä–∞–º–æ—Ç–Ω–æ, –∏ –≤–æ—Ç –Ω–∞—à–µ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ç–∏–ø–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä–Ω–æ –∫ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–º—É
  –∂–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç—É –ø—Ä–∏—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç.

  –ù–æ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ –ª–∏—à—å —á–µ–≥–æ? –¢–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –±–µ—Ä–∏ –ø–æ —Ç–æ–º—É –ø–ª–∞–Ω—É –∏ –¥–µ–ª–∞–π, –¥–µ—Ç–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–π. –î–∞, –Ω—É –Ω–∞—à –∫–∞–∫ –±—É–¥—Ç–æ –¥–∞–∂–µ –±–æ–ª–µ–µ
  —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–æ–∑–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π, —Ä–∞—Å–∫–∏–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∏ –ø–æ—Ö—É–∂–µ, —á–µ–º —É –Ω–∏—Ö. –£ –Ω–∏—Ö —É–∂–µ –≤–æ–æ–±—â–µ –≤—Å–µ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–Ω–æ –±—ã–ª–æ, —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ–Ω–∏ –≤–æ—Ç –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∏–ª–∏ 6000 —á–∞—Å–æ–≤, –∞ –º—ã
  —Ç–∏–ø–∞ –ø–æ–ª—Ç–æ—Ä—ã. –î–∞, –Ω–æ —Å —Ö–µ—Ä–∞–ª–∏ –Ω–∞–¥–æ –∂–µ –≤–æ—Ç —Ä–∞—Å–∫–∏–¥—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å, –¥–µ—Ç–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å?

  –í–æ—Ç —è –¥—É–º–∞—é, —á—Ç–æ —Å—É–ø–µ—Ä –∫—Ä—É—Ç–æ–π –µ—â–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç. –°–µ–π—á–∞—Å —Ç–∞–∫–∞—è –∏–¥–µ—è –º–Ω–µ –≤ –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤—É –ø—Ä–∏—à–ª–∞: —ç—Ç–æ –≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç—É —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—É—é –æ–Ω–∏
  —Ö–æ—Ç–µ–ª–∏, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –ø–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å —Å–∫—Ä–∏–Ω—à–æ—Ç—ã –≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç–∏—Ö –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤, –∞–¥–º–∏–Ω–∞, –∫–∞–∫ –∫–æ–≥–æ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ, –∏ –ø—Ä—è–º —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –∫–∞–∫–æ–π-—Ç–æ –æ–¥–∏–Ω-–¥–≤–∞
  –¥–∏–∑–∞–π–Ω–∞ –≤ Figma. –≠—Ç–æ –∂–µ, –Ω—É —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–Ω–æ –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä—è, —Ç–∞–º —Ç—Ä–∏ —á–∞—Å–∞, –∞ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç —É–∂–µ —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ –∫–ª–∏–∫–∞–±–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ, —Ç–∏–ø–∞ –∫–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–æ –≤—ã–≥–ª—è–¥–∏—Ç. –•–æ—Ç—è —ç—Ç–æ
  –Ω–µ —Ç—Ä–∏ —á–∞—Å–∞, –∏ —Ç—ã –∂–µ –±—É–¥–µ—à—å –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–º—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å —Ç—É–¥–∞-—Å—é–¥–∞, –ø—Ä–æ–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å, –∏ –Ω–∞ –¥–µ–Ω—å –∑–∞–π–º–µ—Ç —Ç–∞–º, –≤–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–∏ 6 —á–∞—Å–æ–≤. –ù–æ —ç—Ç–æ —Ç–∏–ø–∞ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ
  –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –∫–∞–∫ —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–π, —Ç–∏–ø–∞ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–æ—Ç–∏–ø.

  –¢–∏–ø–∞ –æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω–∏—Ç—å: —Å–ª—É—à–∞–π, –Æ—Ä–∏–π, —Ç—ã –∑–Ω–∞–µ—à—å, —á—Ç–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã–µ –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥—ã. –í–æ—Ç –µ—Å—Ç—å waterfall, –≥–¥–µ –º—ã –≤—Å–µ –≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–ª–∏, –Ω–æ –º—ã –∂–µ
  —Ö–æ—Ç–∏–º Scrum, Agile, —Ç—ã –∂–µ —Ö–æ—á–µ—à—å –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–µ–µ –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ. –í–æ—Ç –µ–º—É –Ω–µ —Ç–æ —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –Ω–∞ —É—à–∏ –ø—Ä–∏—Å–µ—Å—Ç—å, –Ω–æ –≤–æ—Ç –æ–Ω —Ç–∏–ø–∞... –ò –≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç—É —à—Ç—É–∫—É
  —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å ‚Äî –æ–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞ —Å–∞–º–æ–º –¥–µ–ª–µ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–∞, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ UX –æ–Ω —Ç–æ–∂–µ –ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–µ–Ω —Å —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã—Ö —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω.
  –†–∞—Å–∫–æ–≤—ã—Ä—è—Ç—å, —Ç—ã —Ç–∞–º –≤–∏–¥–∏—à—å –≤ –ø–æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ—Ç–Ω—É—é —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ user stories, —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –∫–µ–π—Å—ã, –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—ã, –≤–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å—ã, –∞ –∫–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç, –∏ —É
  –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ —Ç–∞–º. –ö–ª–∞—Å—Å–Ω–æ, —ç—Ç–æ –≤–æ–æ–±—â–µ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å.

  –ù–æ –µ—Å–ª–∏ —Ç–∞–º –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ø–æ–ø–∞—Å—Ç—å –≤–æ –≤—Å–µ —ç—Ç–∏ –∞–¥–º–∏–Ω–∫–∏, –Ω–∞ —Å–∫—Ä–∏–Ω—à–æ—Ç–µ —ç—Ç–∏ –≤–æ–æ–±—â–µ —Å–∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å ‚Äî –æ—Ñ–∏–≥–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ, —ç—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –∫—Ä—É—Ç–æ–π
  –Ω–∏–Ω–¥–∑—è-—à–ø–∏–æ–Ω–∞–∂ –ø—Ä—è–º–æ. –Ø –ø—Ä–∏–¥—É–º–∞–ª –∫—Ä—É—Ç—É—é –∏–¥–µ—é, –≤ –≤–æ—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–≥–µ –æ—Ç –Ω–µ–µ. –ù–æ, –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç, –¥–∞–≤–∞–π –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏–∫—É, –µ—Å–ª–∏ —è –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–∞–≤, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ —è –Ω–µ
  —Ç–æ —á—Ç–æ —Ö–æ—á—É ‚Äî —è –∫–∞–∫ —Ä–∞–∑ –Ω–µ —Ö–æ—á—É –∑–∞–±–ª—É–¥–∏—Ç—å—Å—è. –ú–Ω–µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω —Å–µ–Ω—å–æ—Ä, —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç, –Ω–∞—Å—Ç–∞–≤–Ω–∏–∫, —É—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å, –∫–æ—É—á, second opinion, evaluator.
  –¢–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –Ω–µ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞, –∞ –ø—Ä–∞–≥–º–∞—Ç–∏–∫, —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç, –∏–Ω–∂–µ–Ω–µ—Ä —Å —É—á–µ—Ç–æ–º —Ç–∏–ø–∞ —Å–∞–¥–∂–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤, –∫–∞–∫ –≤–æ—Ç –¥—Ä—É–≥ —Ç–∞–º, –ø–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—à—å? –¢–∞–∫, –Ω—É —Ç–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å —Å
  —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã—Ö —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω. –î–∞, –Ω—É –∏–ª–∏ –∫–∞–∫ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ —è –Ω–µ –≤–∏–∂—É.

  –î–∞–ª—å—à–µ, —á—Ç–æ —è –µ—â–µ —Ö–æ—Ç–µ–ª –æ—Ç–º–µ—Ç–∏—Ç—å –ø–æ–º–∏–º–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—ã–¥—É—â–µ–π –º—ã—Å–ª–∏: –ø—Ä–æ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏–∫—É –∏ –ø—Ä–æ –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥ —è —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª, –Ω–æ —á—Ç–æ –±—ã–ª–æ –∑–∞–±—ã—Ç–æ –ø–æ
  –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏. –° —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ —è —Ç—Ä–µ–±—É—é –æ–±—è–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –≤—Å–µ–≥–¥–∞ –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–µ –º–æ–µ –∞—É–¥–∏–æ, —Ç–∞–º –æ–≥—Ä–æ–º–Ω–æ–µ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –ø—É–Ω–∫—Ç–æ–≤, –ø–æ–¥–ø—É–Ω–∫—Ç–æ–≤ ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ
  –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –±—ã—Ç—å —á–µ–∫–±–æ–∫—Å–∞–º–∏ –∏ –ø—Ä–æ–Ω—É–º–µ—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ, —Ç–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å 1, 2, 3, 4 –∏ –∑–Ω–∞—á–æ–∫ Markdown —á–µ–∫–±–æ–∫—Å–∞, –¥–µ—Ñ–∏—Å—ã –∏ –∫–≤–∞–¥—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω—ã–µ —Å–∫–æ–±–∫–∏.

  –ê –µ—Å–ª–∏ —ç—Ç–æ –æ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å–∏—Ç—Å—è –∫ —á–µ–º—É-—Ç–æ, –∫–∞–∫–æ–µ-—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å, —Ç–∏–ø–∞ –¥–∞, traceability –∏ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å parent-child –∏–ª–∏ –¥–≤–æ–π–Ω—É—é, —Ç—Ä–æ–π–Ω—É—é
  –≤–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å, —Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ, —Å—Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –∏ –≤–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å. –ê –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –ø–æ –æ—á–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∏ –≤—Å–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—å –∏ –æ—Ç–º–µ—á–∞—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–Ω–æ, —á—Ç–æ –Ω–µ—Ç,
  –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ —è –¥–∞—é –æ–≥—Ä–æ–º–Ω–æ–µ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–π. –Ø —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –ø–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞—é, —á—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ evaluation –∑–∞–±—ã–ª–∏, –ø—Ä–æ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ –∑–∞–±—ã–ª–∏, –∏ —ç—Ç–æ
  –Ω–∏–∫—É–¥–∞ –Ω–µ –≥–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è, –Ω–∞–¥–æ –Ω–µ –∑–∞–±—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å.

  –°–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–µ–µ: —è –ø—Ä–æ–¥–æ–ª–∂–∞—é —á–∏—Ç–∞—Ç—å –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç—ã, –¥–∞–∂–µ –≤—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–≥–æ –∞–≥–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ —Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä—é. –°–µ–π—á–∞—Å –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä—é —Å–≤–æ—é –∞—É–¥–∏–æ–∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –±—ã–ª–æ
  —ç—Ç–∏—Ö —á–µ–∫–±–æ–∫—Å–æ–≤, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –±—ã —è –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–ª. –Ø –≤–æ—Ç, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –≤—Å–µ —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–∞–≥–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∏–≤–∞—é, —Å—Ç—Ä–∏–º–∏–Ω–≥ –≤—Ä–æ–¥–µ –±—ã —É–º–Ω–æ, —á–µ—Ç–∫–æ, –ø—Ä–∞–≥–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ, –∞ –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º
  –æ–Ω–∞ —É –º–µ–Ω—è –∑–∞–±—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è. –í–æ—Ç —è, –∫–∞–∫ —É–¥–∏–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ, —Å–∞–º –º—ã—Å–ª—é, –∫–∞–∫ LLM: –Ω–∞ –ª–µ—Ç—É —è —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–æ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä—é, –∞ –≤–æ—Ç –≤–∑—è—Ç—å, –≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –∏–ª–∏ –≤–∑—è—Ç—å
  –µ—â–µ —Ä–∞–∑ ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–∞–¥–æ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –∫–æ–º–ø—å—é—Ç–µ—Ä–∞ –≤ –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–µ.

  –¢–∞–∫, –º—ã—Å–ª—å –∫–∞–∫–∞—è? –ù—É –¥–∞, –Ω–µ—Å–æ–º–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω–æ, —Ç–∞–º –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω—ã, C4 –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ –º—ã –≤—Å–µ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–µ–º. –ù—É, –∫–∞–∫-—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è,
  –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤. –í –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø–µ, –≤–æ—Ç —á—Ç–æ —è —Ö–æ—Ç–µ–ª —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç—å –∏ –∑–∞–±—ã–ª, –ø—Ä–∏—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –ø—Ä–æ–ª–∏—Å—Ç—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å, –≤–æ—Ç —Ç–∞–∫ –≤–æ—Ç –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –≤—Å–ª—É—Ö –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ-—Ç–æ
  –º—ã—Å–ª–∏, –∏ –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≤—Å–ø–æ–º–∏–Ω–∞–µ—à—å.

  –í–æ–æ–±—â–µ, –æ–≥—Ä–æ–º–Ω—É—é —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—É, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—É—é —è –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—É—é –ø—Ä–æ–¥–µ–ª–∞–ª, —ç—Ç–æ —Ä–µ—Å–µ—Ä—á. –î–≤–∞ —Ä–µ—Å–µ—Ä—á–∞ –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏—Ö, –¥–∞, –∏ —Ç–∞–º –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑—ã –≤—Å–µ—Ö –∞—Ä—Ç–µ—Ñ–∞–∫—Ç–æ–≤, —Ç–æ
  –µ—Å—Ç—å –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π, –¥–∞, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º —Ä–µ—Å–µ—Ä—á –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ, –∏ —Ç–∞–º –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è, –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ-—Ç–æ –¥–µ—Ç–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏. –†–µ—Å–µ—Ä—á –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ
